msg:Guilin! Life Hotel! It's worth crying. I don't want to check outüò≠

This time in Guilin, I chose to stay at the Lijiang Boya Hotel. Let me first talk about the service. It's really considerate and enthusiastic. As soon as I arrived on the first floor, there was a clerk to greet me, help me with my luggage, and guide me to the hotel lobby on the 13th floor.

As soon as I got to the 13th floor of the hotel, there was a guide to avoid pitfalls at the elevator entrance. Hahahaha, this is simply to help you prepare all the strategies.

There are also various daily necessities prepared next to it: mosquito repellent, Band-Aids, dental floss, cotton swabs, makeup remover, sunscreen, hair styling spray... It's just a treasure box.

The high-altitude scenery on the 13th floor is good. There is also a buffet breakfast and afternoon tea here. Eat delicious food, look at the scenery, and feel happy.

After going up the spiral staircase to the 14th floor, the scenery is very charming. The landscape and city of Guilin are in full view, and you can enjoy the broad vision. You can really enjoy the beautiful scenery without climbing the mountain!

The room is also very clean and comfortable, with a warm decoration style. It's really a good mood to wake up and see the beautiful scenery.

The hotel also has complete facilities, including laundry room, gym, children's playground, swimming pool and other hotel facilities.

Since the hotel is very popular, it may be difficult to book a room here, so it is recommended to plan in advance

msg:Due to the sudden epidemic, we had to change the itinerary and temporarily rebooked the hotel. The booking was very hasty. We could only choose a hotel with a high score and an inexpensive price. The score is still very objective.
First of all, the location of the hotel is good. We drive to various attractions, go to the hospital for nucleic acid testing, and go to popular restaurants within a ten-minute drive. There are also many supermarkets and restaurants around the hotel, which is very convenient. And dining at the hotel's 13th-floor restaurant can enjoy stunning mountain views.
Secondly, what this hotel gives me is that the service is very user-friendly. The hotel does not follow the luxury style of a resort hotel, but it covers all aspects of daily needs and thinks very well for guests. Self-service laundry and robot meal delivery meet the holiday needs under the epidemic. .
Thirdly, although the breakfast in the hotel is not very diverse, the nutrition is well matched, and the price-performance ratio is very high. The quality even exceeds the breakfast price of 128 in my last Intercontinental Hotel.
There are a few small problems. One is that the parking space is a bit tight. Although there are parking spaces every day, sometimes when I come back late, there is really only one parking space that is very difficult to park. I don‚Äôt know if there will be enough in the peak season of summer. . Another is that the two elevators do not seem to be linked, so each time you take the elevator, you need to wait a few minutes. If they can be linked together, it should be more efficient. There is only one chair in the family room, so it is a bit inconvenient to have to change into clean clothes and sit on the bed every time you go back to the room.
